function show_text_register()
{
    jQuery('#label_login').html('укажите e-mail:');
    jQuery('#label_password').html('придумайте пароль:');
    jQuery('#button_enter').html('Зарегистрироваться');
    jQuery('#text_ulogin').html('Вы можете зарегистрироваться через свой профиль:');

    jQuery('#user_login_message').html( '' );
    jQuery('#user_password_message').html( '' );

    jQuery('#href_modal_enter').removeClass('modal_headline_on');
    jQuery('#href_modal_register').addClass('modal_headline_on');

    jQuery('#id_user_action').val( "register" );

    return true;
}
function show_text_enter()
{
    jQuery('#label_login').html('e-mail:');
    jQuery('#label_password').html('пароль:');
    jQuery('#button_enter').html('Войти');
    jQuery('#text_ulogin').html('Вы можете войти через свой профиль:');

    jQuery('#user_login_message').html( '' );
    jQuery('#user_password_message').html( '' );

    jQuery('#href_modal_enter').addClass('modal_headline_on');
    jQuery('#href_modal_register').removeClass('modal_headline_on');

    jQuery('#id_user_action').val( "login" );

    return true;
}
function get_str_form()
{
    var str_html = '';

    str_html = str_html + '<div id="script_div" class="contact-overlay">';
    str_html = str_html + '<div class="contact-container">';
    str_html = str_html + '<div style="height:320px;" class="contact-content">';

    str_html = str_html + '<div class="contact-top"></div>';

    str_html = str_html + '<div style="padding:10px 10px;">';

    str_html = str_html + '<form id="form_auth_modal" method="post" action="">';
    str_html = str_html + '<input type="hidden" id="id_user_action" name="user_action" value = "login" />';

    str_html = str_html + '<h1><a href="" onclick="show_text_enter(); return false;" class="modal_headline_on" id="href_modal_enter">Вход</a> / <a href="" onclick="show_text_register(); return false;" id="href_modal_register">Регистрация</a></h1>';

    str_html = str_html + '<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="margin:30px 0px;">';

    str_html = str_html + '<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">';
    str_html = str_html + '<label for="contact-message" id="label_login" style="width:170px;text-align:right;">e-mail:</label>';
    str_html = str_html + '</td><td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:10px;">';
        str_html = str_html + '<input type="text" id="user_login" class="contact-input" style="width:240px;" />';
    str_html = str_html + '<div id="user_login_message" style="color:#D76300;"></div>';
    str_html = str_html + '</td></tr>';

    str_html = str_html + '<tr><td style="vertical-align:top;">';
    str_html = str_html + '<label for="contact-message" id="label_password" style="width:170px;text-align:right;">пароль:</label>';
    str_html = str_html + '</td><td style="vertical-align:top;padding-bottom:10px;">';
        str_html = str_html + '<input type="password" id="user_password" class="contact-input" style="width:240px;" />';
    str_html = str_html + '<div id="user_password_message" style="color:#D76300;"></div>';
    str_html = str_html + '</td></tr>';

    return str_html;
}
function mark_object( int_id_base, int_id_object )
{
        var str_url = '/ajax/cabinetmark/';
        var str_favorite_value = jQuery( '#favorite_value' + int_id_object ).val();

        if ( str_favorite_value == 0 ) {
                mark_object_set_on( int_id_object );
                int_flag = 1;
        }
        else {
                mark_object_set_off( int_id_object );
                int_flag = 2;
        }

    _global_int_id_base = int_id_base;
    _global_int_id_object = int_id_object;

        jQuery.post( str_url, { int_id_base: int_id_base, int_id_object: int_id_object, int_flag: int_flag }, function( dataJSON ) {

                // set amount favorites
                jQuery( '#mark_total' ).text( dataJSON.int_total );

                if ( dataJSON.int_result == 1 ) {
                }
                else {
                        mark_object_set_off( int_id_object );

            var str_html = get_str_form();
            str_html = str_html + '<tr><td>';
            str_html = str_html + '</td><td>';
            str_html = str_html + '<button type="button" class="contact-send contact-button" tabindex="1004" onclick="cabinet_login( jQuery(\'#user_login\').val(), jQuery(\'#user_password\').val(), function() { mark_object( \'' + int_id_base + '\', \'' + int_id_object + '\' ); } )" id="button_enter">Войти</button>';
            str_html = str_html + '</td></tr>';
            str_html = str_html + '</table>';
            str_html = str_html + '</form>';

            var script_tag = document.createElement('script');
                        script_tag.setAttribute( 'type', 'text/javascript' );
                        script_tag.setAttribute( 'src', 'http://ulogin.ru/js/ulogin.js' );

            str_html = str_html + '<div>';
            str_html = str_html + '<span id="text_ulogin">Вы можете войти через свой профиль:</span><br />';
            str_html = str_html + '<div id="uLogin" x-ulogin-params="callback=ulogin_callback;display=panel;fields=first_name,last_name;providers=vkontakte,odnoklassniki,mailru,facebook,twitter,google,yandex,livejournal,openid;hidden=other;redirect_uri="></div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            // simple modal
            jQuery.modal( str_html, {
                    closeHTML: "<a href='#' title='Закрыть окно' class='modal-close'>x</a>",
                    position: ["30%"],
                    overlayId: "contact-overlay",
                    containerId: "contact-container",
                    onShow: function (dialog) {
                        document.getElementById( 'script_div' ).appendChild( script_tag );
                    }
                }
            );
                }
        }, "json" );

        return true;
}
function subscribe_send()
{
    var datastring = jQuery("#form_subscribe_modal").serialize();
    var vars = datastring.split("&");
    var id = '';
    vars.forEach(function(item, i, vars) {
        vars0 = item.split("=");
        if (vars0[0]=='id' && vars0[1]>0) {
        id=vars0[1];
        }
        if (vars0[0]=='issubscribenewbuilding' && vars0[1]==1) {
            //alert('есть подписка');
            jQuery.ajax({
                url: '/ajax/mycabinet/?action=contentsubscribe&a=0&id=0&idbase=40',
                type: "GET",
                success: function () {
                        alert_modal( "Подписка сохранена.\nМы уведомим вас о появлении новых объектах." );
                }
            });
        }
        if (vars0[0]=='isnewbuilding' && vars0[1]>0) {
                var ajax = function() {
                        jQuery.ajax({
                        url: '/ajax/mycabinet/?action=paidquery&a=1&id=' + id + '&idbase=' + vars0[1],
                        type: "GET",
                        success: function () {
                                alert_modal( "Запрос сохранен.\nМы уведомим вас о появлении новых объектов по этому запросу." );
                        }
                        });
                };
                if (vars0[1]==41) {
                        jQuery( '#save-query' ).attr("href", "/cabinet/buyer/query/").removeAttr("onclick")
                        jQuery( '#save-query span' ).removeClass("icon_save").addClass("icon_save_no")
                        jQuery( '#save-query em' ).html("Запрос<br>сохранён")
                }
                if (vars0[1]==42) {
                        jQuery( '#save-subscribe' ).attr("href", "/cabinet/buyer/subscribe/").removeAttr("onclick")
                        jQuery( '#save-subscribe span' ).removeClass("icon_save").addClass("icon_save_no")
                        jQuery( '#save-subscribe em' ).html("Вы подписаны")
                }


        }
    });
    jQuery.modal.close();
}
function ban_send()
{
    var str_url = '/ajax/cabinetban/';
    var datastring = jQuery("#form_ban_modal").serialize();
    jQuery.ajax({
        type: "POST",
        url: str_url,
        data: datastring,
        dataType: "json",
        success: function(data) {
            if (data.int_count > 0) {
                if (data.int_count & 1) {
                    jQuery('#tr_' + data.id_object).addClass('hide_object');
                }
                if (data.int_count & 2) {
                    jQuery('.agent_' + data.id_agent).each(function() {
                      jQuery(this).addClass('hide_agent');
                    });
                }
                if (data.int_count & 4) {
                    jQuery('.agency_' + data.id_agency).each(function() {
                      jQuery(this).addClass('hide_agency');
                    });
                }
                if (data.int_count & 8) {
                    jQuery('.street_' + data.id_street).each(function() {
                      jQuery(this).addClass('hide_address');
                    });
                }
                if (jQuery('#ban' + data.id_object + '_fullinfo')) {
                    jQuery('#ban' + data.id_object + '_fullinfo').html('скрыт');
                    jQuery('#ban' + data.id_object + '_fullinfo').attr("href", "/cabinet/block/");
                    jQuery('#ban' + data.id_object + '_fullinfo').attr("onclick", "");
                }
            }
            jQuery.modal.close();
//        },
//        error: function(){
//              alert('error handing here');
        }
    });
}

            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            // simple modal
            jQuery.modal( str_html, {
                closeHTML: "<a href='#' title='Закрыть окно' class='modal-close'>x</a>",
                position: ["30%"],
                overlayId: "contact-overlay",
                containerId: "contact-container"
            });
        }
        else {
            var str_html = get_str_form();
            str_html = str_html + '<tr><td>';
            str_html = str_html + '</td><td>';
            str_html = str_html + '<button type="button" class="contact-send contact-button" tabindex="1004" onclick="cabinet_login( jQuery(\'#user_login\').val(), jQuery(\'#user_password\').val(), function() { ban_object( \'' + int_id_base + '\', \'' + int_id_object + '\', \'' + int_id_agent + '\', \'' + int_id_agency + '\', \'' + int_id_street + '\', \'' + id_house + '\', \'' + id_korpus + '\', \'' + id_litera + '\' ) } )" id="button_enter">Войти</button>';
            str_html = str_html + '</td></tr>';
            str_html = str_html + '</table>';
            str_html = str_html + '</form>';

            var script_tag = document.createElement('script');
            script_tag.setAttribute( 'type', 'text/javascript' );
            script_tag.setAttribute( 'src', 'http://ulogin.ru/js/ulogin.js' );

            str_html = str_html + '<div>';
            str_html = str_html + '<span id="text_ulogin">Вы можете войти через свой профиль:</span><br />';
            str_html = str_html + '<div id="uLogin" x-ulogin-params="callback=ulogin_callback;display=panel;fields=first_name,last_name;providers=vkontakte,odnoklassniki,mailru,facebook,twitter,google,yandex,livejournal,openid;hidden=other;redirect_uri="></div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            // simple modal
            jQuery.modal( str_html, {
                closeHTML: "<a href='#' title='Закрыть окно' class='modal-close'>x</a>",
                position: ["30%"],
                overlayId: "contact-overlay",
                containerId: "contact-container",
                onShow: function (dialog) {
                    document.getElementById( 'script_div' ).appendChild( script_tag );
                }
            });
        }
    }, "json" );

    return true;
}
function cabinet_login( str_login, str_password, callback )
{
    var int_function_result = 0;
    var str_url = '/ajax/cabinetlogin/';
    var int_send_query = 1;

    if ( str_login == '' ) {
        int_send_query = 0;
        jQuery('#user_login_message').html( 'не указан логин' );
    }
    else {
        jQuery('#user_login_message').html( '' );
    }

    if ( str_password == '' ) {
        int_send_query = 0;
        jQuery('#user_password_message').html('не указан пароль');
    }
    else {
        jQuery('#user_password_message').html( '' );
    }

    var str_action = jQuery('#id_user_action').val();

    if ( int_send_query == 1 ) {
        jQuery.post( str_url, { str_login: str_login, str_password: str_password, str_action: str_action }, function( dataJSON ) {
            if ( dataJSON.int_result == 1 ) {
                jQuery.modal.close();
                //int_function_result = 1; - никогда не сработает
                                if(callback) callback()
            }
            else { // error
                if ( dataJSON.int_error == 3 ) {
                    jQuery('#user_login_message').html('не указан логин');
                }
                else if ( dataJSON.int_error == 4 ) {
                    jQuery('#user_password_message').html('не указан пароль');
                }
                else if ( dataJSON.int_error == 2 ) {
                    jQuery('#user_password_message').html('неправильный пароль');
                }
                else if ( dataJSON.int_error == 6 ) {
                    jQuery('#user_login_message').html('неправильный формат email');
                }
                else {
                    //alert_modal( dataJSON.str_error, 'Ошибка' );
                    jQuery('#user_password_message').html(dataJSON.str_error);
                }
            }
        }, "json" );
    }

    return int_function_result;
}
function ulogin_callback( str_token )
{
     ulogin( str_token, 'ulogin_callback_result' );

    return true;
}
function ulogin_callback_query( str_token )
{
    ulogin( str_token, 'ulogin_callback_query_result' );

    return true;
}
function ulogin_callback_result()
{
    mark_object( _global_int_id_base, _global_int_id_object );
    jQuery.modal.close();

    return;
}
function ulogin_callback_query_result()
{
    save_query( _global_int_amount, _global_int_id_base, _global_str_query, _global_str_text, _global_str_module );
    jQuery.modal.close();

    return;
}
function ulogin( str_token, str_func_name )
{
    var int_result = 0;

    jQuery.ajax({
        url: 'http://ulogin.ru/token.php',
        type: 'GET',
        dataType:'jsonp',
        data: {'token': str_token, 'host': encodeURIComponent(location.toString())},
            success: function (jqXHR){
                o = eval( "(" + jqXHR + ")" );
                //h_obj = JSON.parse( jqXHR );
                //alert( h_obj.network );
                //alert( h_obj.identity );

                var str_url = '/ajax/cabinetlogin/ulogin/';
                jQuery.post( str_url, { str_login: o.identity, str_password: o.network, str_fname: o.first_name, str_lname: o.last_name }, function( dataJSON ) {
                    f = eval( str_func_name );
                    f();
                    if ( dataJSON.int_result == 1 ) {
                        int_result = 1;
                    }
                    else { // error
                        alert_modal( dataJSON.str_error, 'Ошибка' );
                    }
                }, "json" );
            },
            complete: function( jqXHR, status ){
                //console.log(status);
            }
    });

    return int_result;
}
function mark_object_set_on( int_id_object )
{
        jQuery( '#href' + int_id_object ).text( 'убрать из корзины' );
        jQuery( '#href' + int_id_object ).attr( 'class', 'href_mark_on' );
        jQuery( '#favorite' + int_id_object ).addClass('cart-on').removeClass('cart-off');
    jQuery( '#favorite_value' + int_id_object ).val(1);

    jQuery( '#href' + int_id_object + '_fullinfo' ).text( 'убрать из корзины' );
    jQuery( '#li' + int_id_object + '_fullinfo' ).attr( 'class', 'emls_tab_last emls_tab_last_on' );

        return true;
}
function mark_object_set_off( int_id_object )
{
        jQuery( '#href' + int_id_object ).text( 'в корзину' );
        jQuery( '#href' + int_id_object ).attr( 'class', 'href_mark_off' );
        jQuery( '#favorite' + int_id_object ).addClass('cart-off').removeClass('cart-on')
    jQuery( '#favorite_value' + int_id_object ).val(0);

    jQuery( '#href' + int_id_object + '_fullinfo' ).text( 'в корзину' );
    jQuery( '#li' + int_id_object + '_fullinfo' ).attr( 'class', 'emls_tab_last emls_tab_last_off' );

        return true;
}
function save_query( int_amount, int_id_base, str_query, str_text, str_module )
{
        var str_url = '/ajax/cabinetquery/';

    _global_int_amount = int_amount;
    _global_int_id_base = int_id_base;
    _global_str_query = str_query;
    _global_str_text = str_text;
    _global_str_module = str_module;

        jQuery.post( str_url, { int_amount: int_amount, int_id_base: int_id_base, str_query: str_query, str_text: str_text, str_module: str_module }, function( dataJSON ) {
                if ( dataJSON.int_result == 1 ) {

                        //jQuery( '#save-query' ).attr("href", "/cabinet/buyer/query/").removeAttr("onclick")
                        //jQuery( '#save-query span' ).removeClass("icon_save").addClass("icon_save_no")
                        //jQuery( '#save-query em' ).html("Запрос<br>сохранён")

                        //jQuery( '#save-subscribe' ).attr("href", "/cabinet/buyer/subscribe/").removeAttr("onclick")
                        //jQuery( '#save-subscribe span' ).removeClass("icon_save").addClass("icon_save_no")
                        //jQuery( '#save-subscribe em' ).html("Вы подписаны")

                        //jQuery( '#query_total' ).text( dataJSON.int_amount_query );
                        //jQuery( '#save_query_result' ).html( 'запрос <a href="/cabinet/buyer/query/" target="_blank">сохранен</a>' );
                        if ( dataJSON.int_email_checked == 1 ) {

                                var isquestion=0;
                                if (int_id_base != 42 && int_id_base != 41) {
                                        isquestion=1;
                                }

                                if (int_id_base == 41 || int_id_base == 42) {//41-42

                                        var subscribe_status=jQuery.ajax({
                                                url: '/ajax/mycabinet/?action=contentsubscribe&a=2&id=0&idbase=40',
                                                type: "GET",
                                                async: false
                                        }).responseText;

                                        if (subscribe_status==0) {//subscribe_status
                                                var str_html = '';

                                                str_html = str_html + '<div id="script_div" class="contact-overlay">';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<div class="contact-container">';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<div style="height:200px;" class="contact-content">';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<div class="contact-top"></div>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<div style="padding:10px 10px;">';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<form id="form_subscribe_modal" method="post" action="">';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<input type="hidden" name="id" value="'+dataJSON.crc+'">';

                                                str_html = str_html + '<h1>Подписка</h1>';
                                                str_html = str_html + 'Подписаться на новые поступления.';

                                                str_html = str_html + '<table border="0" cellpadding="2" cellspacing="0" style="margin:20px 0px; width: 400px;">';

                                                str_html = str_html + '<tr><td>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<input type="checkbox" name="issubscribenewbuilding" id="issubscribenewbuilding" value="1" checked="checked">';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</td><td>Подписаться на новые дома в разделе новостроек</td></tr>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<tr><td>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<input type="checkbox" name="isnewbuilding" id="isnewbuilding" value="1" checked="checked">';
                                                if (int_id_base == 41) str_html = str_html + '</td><td>Подписаться на новые поступления по запросу</td></tr>';
                                                if (int_id_base == 42) str_html = str_html + '</td><td>Подписаться на новые поступления в данном доме</td></tr>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<tr><td>';

                                                str_html = str_html + '<tr><td>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</td><td style="text-align: right;">';
                                                str_html = str_html + '<button type="button" onclick="subscribe_send();" class="contact-send contact-button" tabindex="1004" id="button_enter" style="margin-top: 15px;">Сохранить</button>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</td></tr>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</table>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</form>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</div>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</div>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</div>';
                                                str_html = str_html + '</div>';

                                                // simple modal
                                                jQuery.modal( str_html, {
                                                        closeHTML: "<a href='#' title='Закрыть окно' class='modal-close'>x</a>",
                                                        position: ["30%"],
                                                        overlayId: "contact-overlay",
                                                        containerId: "contact-container"
                                                });
                                        }
                                        else
                                        {
                                                isquestion=1;
                                        }//subscribe_status

                                }//41-42

                                if (isquestion == 1) {

                                        jQuery( '#save-query' ).attr("href", "/cabinet/buyer/query/").removeAttr("onclick")
                                        jQuery( '#save-query span' ).removeClass("icon_save").addClass("icon_save_no")
                                        jQuery( '#save-query em' ).html("Запрос<br>сохранён")

                                        jQuery( '#save-subscribe' ).attr("href", "/cabinet/buyer/subscribe/").removeAttr("onclick")
                                        jQuery( '#save-subscribe span' ).removeClass("icon_save").addClass("icon_save_no")
                                        jQuery( '#save-subscribe em' ).html("Вы подписаны")

                                        jQuery( '#query_total' ).text( dataJSON.int_amount_query );
                                        jQuery( '#save_query_result' ).html( 'запрос <a href="/cabinet/buyer/query/" target="_blank">сохранен</a>' );

                                        var ajax = function() {
                                                jQuery.ajax({
                                                        url: '/ajax/mycabinet/?action=paidquery&a=1&id=' + dataJSON.crc + '&idbase=' + int_id_base,
                                                        type: "GET",
                                                        success: function () {
                                                                alert_modal( "Запрос сохранен.\nМы уведомим вас о появлении новых объектов по этому запросу." );
                                                        }
                                                });
                                        };
                                        if(int_id_base == 42) ajax();
                                        else confirm_modal("Отправлять уведомления о новых объектах по этому запросу на email?", ajax, function() { alert_modal( "Запрос сохранен." ); } );
                                }
                        } else {

                                html_modal( "Запрос сохранен.\nВы можете указать электронную почту для уведомлений о новых объектах по этому запросу.\n<input type='text' id='email_subscribe' value='' style='width: 300px;'>", function() {
                                        jQuery.ajax({
                                                url: '/cabinet/ajax/confirmemail/',
                                                data: 'email='+jQuery('#email_subscribe').val(),
                                                type: "POST",
                                                success: function(answer) {
                                                        if (answer.length>0) {
                                                                alert_modal(answer);
                                                        }
                                                }
                                        });
                                } , "Присылать на указанный адрес", "Закрыть" );
                        }
                }
        else if ( dataJSON.int_error == 1 ) {

            var str_html = get_str_form();

            str_html = str_html + '<tr><td>';
            str_html = str_html + '</td><td>';
            str_html = str_html + '<button type="button" class="contact-send contact-button" tabindex="1004" onclick="cabinet_login( jQuery(\'#user_login\').val(), jQuery(\'#user_password\').val(), function() { save_query( \'' + int_amount + '\', \'' + int_id_base + '\', \'' + str_query + '\', \'' + str_text + '\', \'' + str_module + '\' ) } );" id="button_enter">Войти</button>';
            str_html = str_html + '</td></tr>';
            str_html = str_html + '</table>';
            str_html = str_html + '</form>';

            var script_tag = document.createElement('script');
                        script_tag.setAttribute( 'type', 'text/javascript' );
                        script_tag.setAttribute( 'src', 'http://ulogin.ru/js/ulogin.js' );

            str_html = str_html + '<div>';
            str_html = str_html + '<span id="text_ulogin">Вы можете войти через свой профиль:</span><br />';
            str_html = str_html + '<div id="uLogin" x-ulogin-params="callback=ulogin_callback_query;display=panel;fields=first_name,last_name;providers=vkontakte,odnoklassniki,mailru,facebook,twitter,google,yandex,livejournal,openid;hidden=other;redirect_uri="></div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';
            str_html = str_html + '</div>';

            // simple modal
            jQuery.modal( str_html, {
                                closeHTML: "<a href='#' title='Close' class='modal-close'>x</a>",
                                position: ["30%"],
                                overlayId: "contact-overlay",
                                containerId: "contact-container",
                                onShow: function (dialog) {
                                        document.getElementById( 'script_div' ).appendChild( script_tag );
                                }
                        });
        }
                else { // error
            alert_modal( dataJSON.str_error, 'Ошибка' );
                }
        }, "json" );

        return true;
}

(function() {

/*function log() {
        var x = Array.prototype.join.call(arguments, ", ");

var cabinet = document.getElementById('cabinet-info');

var horisontal = document.getElementById('arrow-horisontal-cabinet');
var slide_left, slide_right;

makeFixed('cabinet-info');

slide_left = horisontal.onclick = function() {
        cabinet.className = 'cabinet-info-small';
        horisontal.onclick = slide_right;
        document.cookie = 'cabinet_width=small;path=/';
        return false;
};

slide_right = function() {
        cabinet.className = 'cabinet-info';
        horisontal.onclick = slide_left;
        document.cookie = 'cabinet_width=ladge;path=/';
        return false;
};


if(getCookie('cabinet_width') == 'small') slide_left();

})()
</script>
